9/23/23, 08:39 - Yadhu: Dear ASIET Hackathon Registered Participants,

We are excited to announce that the final evaluation of the ASIET Hackathon is scheduled to take place on 25th and 26th September 2023.

Presentation Time Slot Notification: You will receive your presentation time slot on 24th September 2023, following the successful submission of your presentation.

In preparation for the final evaluation, we kindly request that you follow the instructions below:

1.   Presentation Guidelines: The final presentation will consist of a 10-minute presentation followed by a 5-minute Q&A session. Please make sure your presentation is concise, clear, and effectively communicates your solution.

2.       Team Availability: All team members should be available during the presentation slot. While it is not necessary for all team members to present the idea, we encourage all members to be present to answer questions and provide additional insights if needed.

3.       Alignment with Problem Statement: Your proposed idea should align with the problem statement described on the SIH website.

4.       Class Hour Duty Leave: If you require duty leave for class hours on the presentation days (25th and 26th September), you must obtain prior permission from your staff advisors and HODs. Make sure to make these arrangements well in advance to avoid any scheduling conflicts.



PPT Submission:

To facilitate the evaluation process, we kindly request that you prepare a presentation based on the template available on the SIH website. Please upload your final presentation to the designated Google Drive folder no later than 23rd September 2023. The link to the Google Drive folder is provided below:

https://forms.gle/x8mftbkBUKJSwSTJ6

 

Please upload your presentation by the specified deadline to ensure that the evaluation process runs smoothly.

 If you have any questions or need further assistance, please do not hesitate to reach out to the ASIET Hackathon organizing team.



 Thank you for your dedication and hard work throughout this hackathon. We look forward to seeing your innovative solutions in action.


--
Regards,

Albins Paul
Asst. Prof
Dept. of ECE
ASIET, Kalady

Inclusions

Day 1 : Start from Ernakulam railway station by afternoon. Overnight journey to Madgaon in train.

Day 2 : Reach Madgaon by early morning. Then start journey to Dandeli. On arriving at Resort, freshup and breakfast. Then proceed for water activities which includes Kayaking,Rafting,Zorbing. After that visit some nearby sightseeing spots. Then back to resort for Lunch. Then group can spend time in pool and other indoor activities available there. Evening tea & snacks will be provided. Dj and campfire in nigt time. Dinner and overnight stay. 

Day 3 : After breakfast checkout from resort and start journey to Goa. Reach Goa by afternoon. After lunch sightseeing in places like Chapora fort, Vagator beach, Anjuna beach etc. By evening check into resort. Dinner and overnight stay there.

Day 4 : After breakfast, We shall proceed for sightseeing in places like Aguada fort, Sinquerim beach. Then after lunch Baga Beach and Calangute beach.(NB : Water activities can be arranged if required on exra cost). Back to Resort for dinner and overnight stay. Dj can also be arranged on extra cost if required.

Day 5 : After breakfast, checkout from resort and  we shall proceed to Panaji for city shopping, In between lunch. Then visit Old goa churches and Colva beach. Drop by evening at Madgaon railway station.

Day 6 : Reach college by morning.

Breakfast : Puri bhajji/Iddli/Dosa/Vada/Bread jam/tea coffee/cut fruits
Lunch : Veg meals/Fish curry meals/Chicken Biriyani/ghee rice-chicken curry-chicken kebab-chilly gobi/Goan Fish thali/Veg Thali meals
Dinner : Chappathi/Porotta//Fried rice/Chicken Curry/Veg Curry/chicken 65/tandoori chicken/Soup/desserts
